msg:I have not stayed at this hotel for a while and was nicely surprised by the changes. The lobby was just redone and looks beautiful. I was greeted with the usual warm welcome and checked in smoothly. I would like to specifically recognize the front desk for their efforts and I saw many new faces but still great service. Again, I was assigned a room in Tower 1. I asked if I could have a room in Tower 2 but was informed that the rooms are still under renovation. Hope next time I can stay there. The executive lounge is probably my favorite in China. I uploaded a few pictures here of my morning coffee and croissant; even though I went after breakfast hours they were nice enough to offer me a light breakfast and looked after me. They have a really nice selection of tea and Nespresso which I appreciate.  Before going out I went to the gym, which was also recently redone. They have a piece of equipment from Queenax which I think is unusual for a standard hotel gym and I thought a really nice touch. They seem to be adding a new pool outside, just off of the main swimming pool, and a lot of work outdoors in their gardens. 
There is a new Xin Rong Ji next to the hotel front door, hopefully this will be open soon as it‚Äôs a nice addition to the area. And, I noticed just down the street from the Hilton the old Highton hotel is being redeveloped, they have a Tim Horton‚Äôs opening soon which is nice variety to the Starbucks behind the hotel. It‚Äôs nice to see all the improvements in the area as it‚Äôs convenient to the office.

Figures 4 to 9 are housing facilities. In fact, it is the standard of Doubletree by Hilton. The sound insulation of the door is extremely poor, because there is no corridor transition, the noise of the corridor in the morning can directly wake you up.

The bathroom toilet is not recommended for people over 178 in height to live in. The glass door is on the top, and the bathroom door can only be used during the whole process. The reason is that the toilet is too close to the glass door.

Personally, I really don't like this kind of Zhejiang enterprises that started from nothing with empty gloves to invade my living space with hard advertising.
